ACTOR Komachi 31223
{
//$Category "Touhou Characters"
  Tag "Komachi Onozuka"
  floatspeed 8
  Speed 8
  MONSTER
  Health 2300
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  Scale 0.7
  MinMissileChance 160
  Mass 1000
  MeleeThreshold 192
  MeleeRange 64
  +DONTHURTSPECIES
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +BOSS
  +DONTFALL
  //+LOWGRAVITY
  +NEVERRESPAWN
  +NORADIUSDMG
  +DONTMORPH
  +DONTRIP
  +AMBUSH
  +MISSILEMORE
  +NOICEDEATH
  Painchance 5
  Painsound "touhou/pain"
  Seesound ""

  {
  Spawn:
	KMCH A 0
	KMCH A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,5,2,false)
	KMCH A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,5,35)
	KMCH A 2 A_Look
  Idle:
    KMCH BCDEFA 4 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    KMCH ABCDEF 4 A_Chase
	KMCH A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(2048,"See")
	Goto GetOverHere
  GetOverHere:
    KMA1 ABCDEF 3 A_FaceTarget
	KMA1 A 0 A_PrintBold("\c[C4]That distance isn't as far as you think it is!")
	KMA1 GGGGHHHHIIIIJJJJKKKK 1 A_RadiusThrust(-2048,16384,RTF_NOTMISSILE|RTF_NOIMPACTDAMAGE,16384)
	Goto See
  Pain:
    KMCH I 0 A_Pain
    KMCH IJKJI 3
    Goto See
  Melee:
    KMA1 ABCDEF 3 A_FaceTarget
	KMA1 G 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(100,"touhou/komachi/scythe","touhou/komachi/scythe","none")
	KMA1 HIJK 4 A_FaceTarget
	Goto See

	KMCH A 0 A_Jump(128,"AimShot","SpreadShot","AirSpirits","FloorSpirits")
	Goto SpiralAttack

ACTOR KomachiCoin5
{
  Speed 5
  Radius 4
  Height 4
  damage (10)
  Projectile
  -ACTIVATEIMPACT
  -ACTIVATEPCROSS
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	YYEN A 0
	YYEN A 0 A_Jump(255,"LoopRed","LoopSilver","LoopGold")
  LoopRed:
	RYEN A 0 Bright A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1",50)
    RYEN A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Goto LoopRed+1
  LoopSilver:
	WYEN A 0 Bright A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter2",50)
    WYEN A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Goto LoopSilver+1
  LoopGold:
	YYEN A 0 Bright A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter3",50)
    YYEN A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Goto LoopGold+1
  Death:
	YYEN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1",1,"DeathRed")
	YYEN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter2",1,"DeathSilver")
	YYEN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter3",1,"DeathGold")
	Stop
  DeathRed:
	RYEN AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
	Stop
  DeathSilver:
	WYEN AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
	Stop
  DeathGold:
	YYEN AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
	Stop
  }
}

ACTOR KomachiAirSpirit
{
  Radius 5
  Speed 12
  fastspeed 24
  Height 16
  damage (20)
  Projectile
  -ACTIVATEIMPACT
  -ACTIVATEPCROSS
  RenderStyle Add
  DeathSound "touhou/hit2"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	WBL4 A 1 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("KomachiAirSpiritTrail",0,0,0,0,0,frandom(0,3),0,0)
	WBL4 A 0 Bright A_SeekerMissile(0,1)
	WBL4 A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	WBL4 A 1 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("KomachiAirSpiritTrail",0,0,0,0,0,frandom(0,3),0,0)
	WBL4 A 0 Bright A_Weave(frandom(-2,2),frandom(-2,2),frandom(-2.0,2.0),frandom(-1.0,1.0))
	WBL4 A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
    VBL4 AAAAAAAAAA 3 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR KomachiFloorSpirit : KomachiAirSpirit
{
  +FLOORHUGGER
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	WBL4 A 0 Bright A_Jump(1,"StopState")
	WBL4 A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	WBL4 A 1 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("KomachiAirSpiritTrail",0,0,0,0,0,frandom(0,3),0,0)
    Loop
  StopState:
	WBL4 A 0 Bright A_Stop
	WBL4 A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")

ACTOR KomachiAncientEarthboundSpirits : Komachi
{
  Tag "Komachi Onozuka"
  Health 2200
  DropItem "KomachiNS2"
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	KMCH A 0
	KMCH AA 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
    KMCH BBCCDDEEFF 2 A_FadeIn(0.1)
  Idle:
	KMCH ABCDEF 4 A_Look
	Loop
  See:
	KMA2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
	KMA2 KLMN 6 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6104)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6104,2,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6104,35)
	KMA2 A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,47)
	KMA2 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	KMA2 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	KMA2 OPOPOPOPOPOPQRS 3 A_FaceTarget
	KMA2 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	KMA2 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	Goto Missile
  ChaseState:
    KMCH ABCDEF 4 A_Chase
	KMCH A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(2048,"See")
	Goto GetOverHere
  Missile:
	KMCH A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"MissileEasy")
	KMCH A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"MissileNormal")
	KMCH A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"MissileHard")
	KMCH A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"MissileLunatic")
	Goto MissileHard
  MissileEasy:
    KMA1 A 5 A_FaceTarget
    KMA1 BCDEFGHIJK 3 A_CustomBulletAttack(0,0,1,0,"KomachiAncientEarthboundSpiritPuffEasy")
	Goto See
  MissileNormal:
    KMA1 A 5 A_FaceTarget
    KMA1 BCDEFGHIJK 3 A_CustomBulletAttack(0,0,1,0,"KomachiAncientEarthboundSpiritPuffNormal")
	Goto See
  MissileHard:
    KMA1 A 5 A_FaceTarget
    KMA1 BCDEFGHIJK 3 A_CustomBulletAttack(0,0,1,0,"KomachiAncientEarthboundSpiritPuffHard")
	Goto See
  MissileLunatic:
    KMA1 A 5 A_FaceTarget
    KMA1 BCDEFGHIJK 3 A_CustomBulletAttack(0,0,1,0,"KomachiAncientEarthboundSpiritPuffLunatic")
	Goto See
  Death:
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PowerPickup2",0,0,0,frandom(0,6),frandom(0,6),frandom(3,12),frandom(0,360),0,0)
	KMA1 A 0 ACS_Execute(603,0)
	Goto "Super::Death"
	}
}

	KMCH A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6105,1,false)
	KMCH A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6105,35)
	KMCH A 1 A_Look
	KMCH BCDEF 4 A_Look
	Loop
  See:
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6105)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6105,1,false)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6105,35)
	KMA2 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
    KMCH ABCDEF 4 A_Chase
	KMCH A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(2048,"See")
	Goto GetOverHere
  }
}
